<p>Diminutive of <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">borre, borne</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">well, <a href = vnd.unilang:drinkwater.html>drinkwater</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Compare <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:bron.html>bron</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">well</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_3">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

</p>
<ol><li>a <span class="Latn" lang="en">shot</span> of an <span class="Latn" lang="en">alcoholic</span> <a href = vnd.unilang:drink.html>drink</a> such as <span class="Latn" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:rum.html>rum</a></span> or <span class="Latn" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:gin.html>gin</a></span>; a <span class="Latn" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:tot.html>tot</a></span></li>
<li>an <span class="Latn" lang="en">informal</span>, often <span class="Latn" lang="en">impromptu</span> <span class="Latn" lang="en">reception</span> or <span class="Latn" lang="en">meetup</span>, typically involving alcoholic drinks</li></ol>

***borscht.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:borscht.html>borscht</a> (65781)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>1884 or 1808. Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Yiddish" class="extiw" title="w:Yiddish">Yiddish</a></span> <i class="Hebr mention" lang="yi">באָרשט</i> |  <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="yi-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">borsht</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Russian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Russian language">Russian</a></span> or <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ukrainian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Ukrainian language">Ukrainian</a></span> <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="uk">борщ</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="uk-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">boršč</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Doublet of <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">barszcz</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:borscht.html>borscht</a></strong> (<i>countable and uncountable</i>, <i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en">borschts</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>A beetroot soup that can be served hot or cold, usually with sour cream.</li>
<li>Any similar sour soup made of other ingredients such as sorrel, cabbage, hogweed</li></ol>
</body>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:borstbeen.html>borstbeen</a> (28293)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:borstbeen.html>borstbeen</a></i>. <hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:borstbeen.html>borstbeen</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:borstbeen.html>borstbeenderen</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl">borstbenen</b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:borstbeen.html>borstbeentje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)

<ol><li>breastbone, sternum</li></ol>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Zelfstandig_naamwoord"><i><a href = vnd.unilang:zelfstandig.html>Zelfstandig</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:naamwoord.html>naamwoord</a></i></span></h4>
<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:borstbeen.html>borstbeen</a></b> <span style="background-color: f8f9fa;border-radius: 2px;border: 1px solid c8ccd1;padding: 0 0.2em 0 0.1em;font-style: italic"><a href = vnd.unilang:o.html>o</a></span>

***bos.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:bos.html>bos</a> (1456)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_3">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:bosch.html>bosch</a></i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">busch</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*busc</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*buskaz</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_6">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

***boter.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:boter.html>boter</a> (4577)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">bōter</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*butera</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">būtȳrum</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ancient_Greek" class="extiw" title="w:Ancient Greek">Ancient Greek</a></span> <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">βούτυρον</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">boúturon</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:boter.html>boter</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:boter.html>boters</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:boter.html>botertje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>Butter, a spread made from churned milk.</li>
<li>A butter substitute, typically made of vegetable <a href = vnd.unilang:oils.html>oils</a>.</li></ol>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Zelfstandig_naamwoord"><i><a href = vnd.unilang:zelfstandig.html>Zelfstandig</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:naamwoord.html>naamwoord</a></i></span></h4>

***boterham.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:boterham.html>boterham</a> (6867)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Alteration of earlier <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">boteram</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">boterram</i>, of uncertain origin. Possibly from <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:boter.html>boter</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">butter</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">*<a href = vnd.unilang:rammen.html>ramme</a></i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">*<a href = vnd.unilang:remmen.html>remme</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">thick slice of bread</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> (compare obsolete <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:rammel.html>rammel</a></i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">remmel</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">thick slice of bread</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> and <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/West_Flemish" class="extiw" title="w:West Flemish">West Flemish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="vls">rammeke</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">toasted sandwich</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>). Alternatively perhaps from <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:boter.html>boter</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">butter</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">*<a href = vnd.unilang:ham.html>ham</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">chunk</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.<sup id="cite_ref-1" class="reference"><a href="cite_note-1"> | 1 | </a></sup> Alternatively, short for <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">boterenbroot</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">buttered bread</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Unrelated to <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:ham.html>ham</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss"><a href = vnd.unilang:ham.html>ham</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Related to <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Low_German" class="extiw" title="w:Low German">Low German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nds">boteram</i> and <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/French_language" class="extiw" title="w:French language">French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr">bouterame</i>, which are borrowed from the Dutch.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:boterham.html>boterham</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:boterhammen.html>boterhammen</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:boterhammetje.html>boterhammetje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>a slice of bread</li>
<li>sandwich</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related <a href = vnd.unilang:terms.html>terms</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Latn" lang="nl">bammetje</span></li>

***bottel.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:bottel.html>bottel</a> (132879)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">buttel</i>. Equivalent to <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:bot.html>bot</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss"><a href = vnd.unilang:bud.html>bud</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">-el</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:bottel.html>bottel</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:bottel.html>bottels</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:bottel.html>botteltje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="Latn" lang="en">hip</span>, <span class="Latn" lang="en">rosehip</span>
<dl><dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonym:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="nl">rozenbottel</span></span></dd></dl></li>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:botter.html>botter</a> (108598)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From a dialectal variant of <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Dutch_language" class="extiw" title="w:Dutch language">Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:boter.html>boter</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">bōter</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*butera</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">būtȳrum</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ancient_Greek" class="extiw" title="w:Ancient Greek">Ancient Greek</a></span> <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">βούτυρον</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">boúturon</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="af"><a href = vnd.unilang:botter.html>botter</a></strong> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-af p-form-of" lang="af"><a href = vnd.unilang:bot.html>botters</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-af diminutive-form-of" lang="af">bottertjie</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">uncountable</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> <span class="Latn" lang="en">butter</span>; a <span class="Latn" lang="en">soft</span>, <span class="Latn" lang="en">fatty</span> <span class="Latn" lang="en">foodstuff</span> made from the <span class="Latn" lang="en">cream</span> of <span class="Latn" lang="en">milk</span></li>
<li><span class="Latn" lang="en">butter</span> <span class="Latn" lang="en">type</span>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="af"><a href = vnd.unilang:ons.html>Ons</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>het</a> 'n <a href = vnd.unilang:klomp.html>klomp</a> gegeurde <b><a href = vnd.unilang:bot.html>botters</a></b> beskikbaar.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation"><a href = vnd.unilang:we.html>We</a> have a lot of flavoured <b>butter [<a href = vnd.unilang:types.html>types</a>]</b>/<b><a href = vnd.unilang:butters.html>butters</a></b> available.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">chemistry<span class="ib-comma">,</span> dated</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> <span class="Latn" lang="en">butter</span>; any specific soft <span class="Latn" lang="en">substance</span></li></ol>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="af"><a href = vnd.unilang:botter.html>botter</a></strong> (<i>present</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-af pres-form-of" lang="af"><strong class="selflink"><a href = vnd.unilang:botter.html>botter</a></strong></b>, <i>present participle</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-af pres | ptcp-form-of" lang="af">botterende</b>, <i>past participle</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-af past | ptcp-form-of" lang="af">gebotter</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to <span class="Latn" lang="en">butter</span>; to <span class="Latn" lang="en">spread</span> butter</li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:252px;"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/69/Bottermetaap.jpg/250px-Bottermetaap.jpg" decoding="async" width="250" height="174" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/69/Bottermetaap.jpg/375px-Bottermetaap.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/6/69/Bottermetaap.jpg 2x" data-file-width="407" data-file-height="284" />  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"></div><a href = vnd.unilang:botter.html>Botter</a> <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">Dutch fishing vessel</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span>.</div></div></div>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Dutch_language" class="extiw" title="w:Dutch language">Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:botter.html>botter</a></i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_3">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="af"><a href = vnd.unilang:botter.html>botter</a></strong> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-af p-form-of" lang="af"><a href = vnd.unilang:bot.html>botters</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-af diminutive-form-of" lang="af">bottertjie</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>a type of <span class="Latn" lang="en">Dutch</span> <span class="Latn" lang="en">fishing</span> <span class="Latn" lang="en">vessel</span> with a <span class="Latn" lang="en">characteristic</span> <span class="Latn" lang="en">hull</span></li></ol>

***bouillon.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:bouillon.html>bouillon</a> (20135)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/French_language" class="extiw" title="w:French language">French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr"><a href = vnd.unilang:bouillon.html>bouillon</a></i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:bouillon.html>bouillon</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:bouillon.html>bouillons</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:bouillon.html>bouillonnetje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="Latn" lang="en">stock</span>, <span class="Latn" lang="en">broth</span> <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">water in which meat (or other food) <a href = vnd.unilang:has.html>has</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:been.html>been</a> boiled</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span>
<dl><dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonym:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:vleesnat.html>vleesnat</a></span></span></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">dated</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> <span class="Latn" lang="en">bullion</span>, fringe of gold or silver wire
<dl><dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonym:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="nl">cantille</span></span></dd></dl></li></ol>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Zelfstandig_naamwoord"><i><a href = vnd.unilang:zelfstandig.html>Zelfstandig</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:naamwoord.html>naamwoord</a></i></span></h4>

***bouw.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:bouw.html>bouw</a> (4065)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:bouw.html>bouw</a></i>. <span class="maintenance-line"><i>This etymology <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> incomplete. You can help Wiktionary by elaborating on the origins of this term.</i></span>
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:bouw.html>bouw</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>uncountable</i>)
</p>
<ol><li>construction
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>De</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:bouw.html>bouw</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:duurde.html>duurde</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:vijf.html>vijf</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:jaar.html>jaar</a>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">The <b>construction</b> (of a building) lasted five years.</span></dd></dl></div></dd>
<dd><i><a href = vnd.unilang:zij.html>Zij</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:werkt.html>werkt</a> in <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:bouw.html>bouw</a></b>.</i>
<dl><dd>She works in <b>construction</b>.</dd></dl></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">dialectal<span class="ib-comma">,</span> archaic</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> <span class="Latn" lang="en">cultivation</span>, <span class="Latn" lang="en">tillage</span></li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Javanese_language" class="extiw" title="w:Javanese language">Javanese</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="jv">bahu</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Sanskrit" class="extiw" title="w:Sanskrit">Sanskrit</a></span> <i class="Deva mention" lang="sa">बाहु</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="sa-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">bāhu</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:bouw.html>bouw</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:bouw.html>bouws</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">historical</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A unit of measure for area on Java, equivalent to about 0.7 hectare; a portion of agricultural <a href = vnd.unilang:land.html>land</a> of this size.</li></ol>

***bouwheer.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:bouwheer.html>bouwheer</a> (108595)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:bouwen.html>bouwen</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to build</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:heer.html>heer</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">lord</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:bouwheer.html>bouwheer</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:bouwheer.html>bouwheren</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:bouwheer.html>bouwheertje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">historical</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A master mason.</li>
